                        <div data-reactid="1326">
                         Furnished apartment with beautiful view of Brasilia. Floor tall, new building with gym, sauna, swimming pool, gourmet and barbecue. The apartament has one bedroom with bathroom, one living room and kitchen. Next to the metro concessionarias (200 metros), where you have links to the town of Brasilia. Also next to the shopping mall Que ( a very nice place with good bars, restaurants, pizzarias, mcdonalds, supermarket, banks, etc). There is a very nice ecologic park Aguas Claras. The apartament is about 25 minutes to the town of Brasilia (touristics points) by metro. Brasilia has a beautiful architeture by oscar Niemeyer and interestings monuments. There is Internet 10 mega(wi fi) and sky tv. There is a very good bakery next the apartment where you can appreciate our famous pão de queijo with a good brazilian coffee, a delicious from Brazil, very popular!! We can organize transfer from the Airport to the apartament and the apartament to the Airport. And we can also arrange a city tour! We also speak English. You are welcome!!
